The hotel has a large lawn and a parent-child park. I think there is enough space to set up tents in the hotel. I donâ€™t know whether the lawn is rented out separately to camping enthusiasts.
I personally think that the breakfast is relatively rich, with Chongming cakes with Chongming characteristics, and the taste is relatively authentic, but it is a little thin, and the steaming time is a little long, resulting in too soft collapse. For hotels of the same price, compared horizontally, the breakfast is enough to eat, but the category is average.
Overall, I am very satisfied with this accommodation experience.
